SELECT s.bestObjID,s.ra, s.dec, s.z,  s.zWarning, s.class, s.subClass, s.sciencePrimary,   s.survey, s.programname, s.legacy_target1, s.boss_target1, s.eboss_target0,  p.modelMag_u, p.modelMag_g, p.modelMag_r, p.modelMag_i, p.modelMag_z,  p.petroMag_u, p.petroMag_g, p.petroMag_r, p.petroMag_i, p.petroMag_z,  g.dered_u, g.dered_g, g.dered_r, g.dered_i, g.dered_z,  g.petroR5#_u, g.petroR5#_g, g.petroR5#_r, g.petroR5#_i, g.petroR5#_z,  g.petroR9#_u, g.petroR9#_g, g.petroR9#_r, g.petroR9#_i, g.petroR9#_z,  pz.z, pz.lumDist, pz.absMagU, pz.absMagG, pz.absMagR, pz.absMagI, pz.absMagZ FROM PhotoObjAll AS p JOIN specObj AS s ON s.bestObjID = p.objID JOIN Galaxy AS g ON g.objID = p.objID JOIN Photoz as pz ON pz.objID = p.objID WHERE s.ra BETWEEN # AND #  AND s.dec BETWEEN # and #  AND s.class = &&&  AND (boss_target1 & #) != #  AND s.z BETWEEN # and #  AND s.zWarning = # ORDER BY s.z
